# Aws Documentation

Source: https://docs.aws.amazon.com/llms-full.txt

---

# Amazon Web Services (AWS) Documentation
> This file provides structured access to AWS service documentation for large language models. Each section represents a service landing page with links to key documentation resources.

## Guides


- [Amazon Linux 2 Release Notes](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AL2/latest/relnotes/relnotes-al2.html): Find the release notes for Amazon Linux 2, which provide information about new features, updates, and fixes. [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AL2/latest/relnotes/llms.txt)
- [AWS Resource Groups Resource Groups API Reference](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ARG/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html): AWS Resource Groups lets you organize AWS resources such as Amazon Elastic Compute Cloud instances, Amazon Relational Database Service databases, and Amazon Simple Storage Service buckets into groups using criteria that you define as tags.  [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ARG/latest/APIReference/llms.txt)
- [AWS Resource Groups User Guide](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ARG/latest/userguide/resource-groups.html): Learn about AWS Resource Groups and how resource groups can help you organize and manage your AWS resources. [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ARG/latest/userguide/llms.txt)
- [AWS CloudFormation API Reference](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html): AWS CloudFormation allows you to create and manage AWS infrastructure deployments predictably and repeatedly.  [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/APIReference/llms.txt)
- [AWS CloudFormation Template Reference](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/TemplateReference/introduction.html): Find reference information for the resource types, resource properties, resource attributes, intrinsic functions, and transforms that you can use in CloudFormation templates. [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/TemplateReference/llms.txt)
- [AWS CloudFormation User Guide](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/UserGuide/Welcome.html): Use CloudFormation to model, provision, and manage AWS and third-party resources by treating infrastructure as code. [llms.txt](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSCloudFormation/latest/UserGuide/llms.txt)
